<script type="text/javascript">
    var m_ut = (function () {
        var content, isAccept = false;
        function init() {
            if(!isAccept){
                if (readCookie('marmCA') != null) {
                    accept();
                }else{
                    createCookie('marmCA', 'fvis; domain=.marmiton.org');
                }
            }
        }

        function setHtml(){
            content = document.getElementById('m_cookie_popup');
            if(isAccept)
                removeAlert();
            else{
                var btn = document.getElementById("m_cookies-bar-btn");
                m_bindEvent(btn,"click",accept );
                m_bindEvent(window,"scroll",function(e){if(m_Window.st >= 300){accept();}});
            }
        }

        function accept() {
            try {
                if(!isAccept){
                    createCookie('marmCA', 'read; domain=.marmiton.org', 365);
                    isAccept = true;
                    removeAlert();
                }
            }
            catch (ex) {
                if(window.mlog)window.mlog(ex);
            }
        }

        function removeAlert() {
            if(content)
                content.parentElement.removeChild(content);
        }

        function createCookie(name,value,days) {
            var expires = '';
            if (days) {
                var date = new Date();
                date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
                var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
            }
            document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
        }

        function readCookie(name) {
            var nameEQ = name + "=";
            var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
            for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
                var c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
                if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
            }
            return null;
        }

        function eraseCookie(name,domain,path) {
            var cookieValue = name+"=";
            if (domain && domain != '')
                cookieValue += '; domain=' + domain;
            if (path && path != '')
                cookieValue += '; path=' + path;
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime()-10000);
            cookieValue += '; expires='+date.toGMTString();
            document.cookie = cookieValue;
        }

        init();
        return {
            accept: accept
            ,isAccept:function(){return isAccept;}
            ,setHtml:setHtml
        }
    })();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
m_overlay = function () {
    var SEL_OVERLAY = 'j_overlay',
        SEL_TITLE = 'j_title',
        SEL_CONTENT = 'j_content',
        SEL_CLOSE = 'j_close',
        SEL_WRAPPER = 'j_wrapper',
        SEL_INTERCEPT = 'j_intercept',
        SEL_ANSWER = 'j_answer',
        CSS_HIDE = 'm_hide',
        CSS_NOSCROLL = 'm_noscroll',
        COOKIE_OVERLAY = 'MARMIMESSAGE',
        answersHandlers = {
            'cancel': function () {
                close();
                return false;
            },
            'no': function () {
                close();
                return false;
            },
            'ok' : function() {
                close();
                return true;
            },
            'yes': function () {
                close();
                return true;
            }
        },
        sizes = {
            'xsmall': 'wrapper_xs',
            'small': 'wrapper_sm',
            'medium': 'wrapper_md',
            'large': 'wrapper_lg'
        },
        answerCallback,
        overlay,
        wrapper,
        title,
        content,
        answers,
        overlayClass,
        center;

    function init() {
        overlay = getElementsByClassName(SEL_OVERLAY, document)[0];
        wrapper = getElementsByClassName(SEL_WRAPPER, overlay)[0];
        title = getElementsByClassName(SEL_TITLE, overlay)[0];
        content = getElementsByClassName(SEL_CONTENT, overlay)[0];
        answers = getElementsByClassName(SEL_ANSWER, overlay);
        
        setEvents();

        if (readCookie(COOKIE_OVERLAY)) {
            show();
            eraseCookie(COOKIE_OVERLAY);
        }
    }

    function setEvents() {
        var close_bttns = getElementsByClassName(SEL_CLOSE, overlay),
            intercept_elms = getElementsByClassName(SEL_INTERCEPT, overlay),
            i = intercept_elms.length,
            answer,
            data;

        for (; i--;) {
            m_bindEvent(intercept_elms[i], 'click', intercept);
        }

        i = close_bttns.length;
        for (; i--;) {
            m_bindEvent(close_bttns[i], 'click', answerClick(close_bttns[i], answersHandlers.cancel));
        }

        i = answers.length;
        for (; i--;) {
            answer = answers[i];
            data = $(answer).data('answer');
            if (!answersHandlers.hasOwnProperty(data)) continue;

            m_bindEvent(answer, 'click', answerClick(answer));
        }
    }

    function answerClick(elm, handler) {
        var self = this,
            data = $(elm).data('answer');
            handler = handler || answersHandlers[data];

        return function () {
            var result = handler.apply(self, arguments);
            if (answerCallback && typeof answerCallback === 'function') {
                answerCallback(result);
            }

            return result;
        };
    }

    function close(evt) {
        removeClass(document.body, CSS_NOSCROLL);
        AddClass(overlay, CSS_HIDE);
        m_preventDefault(evt);
        if(m_events)m_events.publish("m_overlay-closed", {});
        return false;
    }

    function intercept(evt) {
        m_stopPropagation(evt);

        return false;
    }

    function show(opts, callback) {
        var args = opts || {},
            bttns = args.bttns || [],
            answer,
            answerData,
            i;

        //set the wrapper size
        if (args.size && sizes.hasOwnProperty(args.size)) {
            for (var size in sizes) {
                if (!sizes.hasOwnProperty(size)) continue;

                if (args.size === size) {
                    AddClass(wrapper, sizes[size]);
                }
                else {
                    removeClass(wrapper, sizes[size]);
                }
            }
        }

        //show the requested buttons
        i = answers.length;
        for (; i--;) {
            answer = answers[i];
            answerData = $(answer).data('answer');
            if (bttns.indexOf(answerData) === -1) {
                AddClass(answer, CSS_HIDE);
            }
            else {
                removeClass(answer, CSS_HIDE);
            }
        }

        // add overlay class
        if (args.overlayClass) {
            AddClass(overlay, args.overlayClass);
        }

        //add title
        if (args.title) {
            title.innerHTML = args.title;
        }

        //add content
        if (args.content !== undefined) {
            //TODO : gestion d'un contenu html
            content.innerHTML = "";
            if (typeof (args.content) === "object" && args.content.nodeName) {
                content.appendChild(args.content);
            } else {
                content.innerHTML = args.content
            }
        } else {
           // content.innerHTML = "";
        }

        // center
        if (args.center == false)
            removeClass(content, 'm_text_align_center');
        else if (!hasClass(content, 'm_text_align_center'))
            AddClass(content, 'm_text_align_center');


        if (callback && typeof callback === 'function') answerCallback = callback;

        AddClass(document.body, CSS_NOSCROLL);
        removeClass(overlay, CSS_HIDE);
    }

    init();

    return {
        close: close,
        show: show
    };
}();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    try
    {
        m_bindEvent(window, "message",function (event) {
            if (event.origin.indexOf('marmiton.org') > 0 && event.data == "loginbox") {
                location.reload();
            }
        });
    }
    catch (ex) {
        if (typeof (window.mlog) === "function") { window.mlog(ex, 2); }
    }
    var m_connectBox = (function () {
        var _that = {
            container: null,
            iframeContainer: null,
            isIframeAppend: false
        };
        _that.init = function (containerId, iframeContainerId) {
            _that.container = document.getElementById(containerId);
            _that.iframeContainer = document.getElementById(iframeContainerId);
        }

        _that.open = function () {
            if (_that.container == null)
                return false;
            if (_that.iframeContainer == null)
                return false;
            if (!_that.isIframeAppend) {
                var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
                iframe.width="100%";
                iframe.height="300px";
                iframe.frameBorder="0";
                iframe.scrolling="no";
                iframe.src = 'https://www.marmiton.org/espace-perso/espacepersologiniframe.aspx';
                _that.iframeContainer.appendChild(iframe);
                _that.isIframeAppend = true;
            }

            if (_that.container.className.indexOf("open") < 0) {
                AddClass(_that.container, "open");
                setTimeout(function () { m_bindEvent(window, "click", _that.close); }, 500);
            }
        }

        _that.close = function (e) {
            if (_that.container == null)
                return false;
            var internalClick = false;
            if (typeof e !== "undefefined") {
                var ele = e.srcElement;
                do {
                    if (ele.id == _that.container.id) {
                        internalClick = true;
                    }
                    ele = ele.parentElement;
                } while (ele != null);
            }
            if (!internalClick && _that.container.className.indexOf("open") >= 0) {
                m_unbindEvent(window, "click", _that.close);
                removeClass(_that.container, "open");
            }
        }

        return _that;
    })();

    function m_unbindEvent(elem, eventType, handler) {
        if (elem.removeEventListener)
            elem.removeEventListener(eventType, handler, false);
        if (elem.detachEvent)
            elem.detachEvent('on' + eventType, handler);
    }

    m_connectBox.init("m_box_connect", "m_box_connect_iframe_container");
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $("li.m_nav_opecoca").find("a").addClass('m_nav_opecocaImg');
    });

    function headerDisplay(e) {
        var headerSticky = getElement("#header_sticky");
        var header = getElement("#header");
        var baseline = getElement("#m_accroche_baseline");
        var search = getElement("#m_recherche_sticky");
        var linkcomm = getElement("#m_liens_commerciaux");
        var hamMenu = getElement("#hamburger");
        var menuham = getElement("#m_menu_ham");
        var shareLink = getElement("#m_partage_sticky");
        if (m_Window.scrollTop() > 0 && header.className.indexOf('m_top') < 0) {

            AddClass(headerSticky, "m_sticky");
            
            AddClass(hamMenu, "m_show");
            AddClass(baseline, "m_hide");
            AddClass(linkcomm, "m_hide");
            AddClass(header, "m_top");
        } else if (m_Window.scrollTop() == 0 && header.className.indexOf('m_top') > 0) {
            removeClass(headerSticky, "m_sticky");
            removeClass(menuham, "m_show");
            removeClass(hamMenu, "m_show");
            
                removeClass(baseline, "m_none");
                removeClass(linkcomm, "m_none");
                removeClass(header, "m_top");
                setTimeout(function () { removeClass(baseline, "m_hide"); }, 10);
                removeClass(linkcomm, "m_hide");
                
        }
    }


    function initHeader() {
        m_Window.init();
        m_bindEvent(window, 'scroll', headerDisplay);
        m_bindEvent(window, 'touchend', closeMenuHam);
        m_bindEvent(window, 'click', closeMenuHam);
        var transitionEnd = transitionEndEventName();
        m_bindEvent(getElement("#m_accroche_baseline"), transitionEnd, noneBaseline);
        m_bindEvent(getElement("#m_liens_commerciaux"), transitionEnd, noneLinkcomm);
        headerDisplay();
    }

    function redirectSearch() {
        location.href = 'http://www.marmiton.org/recettes/recherche.aspx?type=all';
    }

    function ctl00_m_CtrlNavigation_SearchGo() {
        ctl00_m_CtrlNavigation_SearchGoCommon(document.getElementById('m_recherche_sticky_text'));
    }

    function ctl00_m_CtrlNavigation_SearchGoCommon(_input) {
        var _keywords = _input.value;
        _keywords = _keywords.replace(/^\s+/g, '').replace(/\s+$/g, '');
        if (_keywords != '' && _keywords != _input.placeholder) {

            var _url = 'http://www.marmiton.org/recettes/recherche.aspx';
            _url += "?s=" + encodeURI(_keywords) + "&type=all";

            if (window !== top) {
                window.open(_url, "_top");
            }
            else {
                document.location = _url;
            }

        }
        else {
            m_overlay.show({ title: "Recherche", content: "Merci de saisir un ingrédient ou le nom d\u0027un plat...", size: "xsmall" });
        }
    }
    m_bindEvent(window, 'load', initHeader);

</script>
<script>
    function m_resize_menu() {
        var itemsNav = document.getElementById('main-menu'),
            _navChildren = itemsNav.children,
            _navChildrenSize = _navChildren.length,
            menuLimit = m_Window.sw - 30,
            menuSize = itemsNav.offsetWidth,
            _newDropDownMenu = '',
            storageItems = '',
            j = _navChildrenSize - 1;
        if (menuSize > menuLimit) {
            menuLimit -= 50; // Space for dropdown menu
            while (menuSize > menuLimit && j >= 0) {
                if (_navChildren[j].getAttribute('id') !== 'dropdown') {
                    var contentChildren = _navChildren[j].querySelector("div").innerHTML;
                    _navChildren[j].style.display = 'none';
                    _newDropDownMenu = '<li>' + contentChildren + '</li>\r\n' + _newDropDownMenu;
                    menuSize = itemsNav.offsetWidth;
                }
                j--;
            }
            if (!document.getElementById('dropdown')) {
                var _wrapper = document.createElement('li');
                _wrapper.id = 'dropdown';
                _wrapper.className = 'm_nav_menu_deroulant';
                _wrapper.innerHTML += '<div><a href="javascript: void(0);"></a></div>';
                _wrapper.innerHTML += '<div id="dropdown-items" class="dropdown-list m_sub_nav m_sub_nav_l"><a class="m_nav_link2" href="javascript: void(0);"></a><ul>' + _newDropDownMenu + '</ul></div>'
                itemsNav.appendChild(_wrapper);
            } else {
                document.getElementById('dropdown-items').getElementsByTagName('ul')[0].innerHTML = _newDropDownMenu;
            }
        } else {
            var i = 0;
            while (i <= j && menuSize < menuLimit) {
                if (_navChildren[i].style.display == 'none') {
                    _navChildren[i].style.display = 'block';
                    if (itemsNav.offsetWidth > (document.body.clientWidth - 80)) {
                        _navChildren[i].style.display = 'none';
                    } else {
                        var element = document.getElementById('dropdown-items').getElementsByTagName('li')[0];
                        element.parentNode.removeChild(element);
                    }
                }
                i++;
            }
            if (document.getElementById('dropdown-items') && !document.getElementById('dropdown-items').getElementsByTagName('li')[0])
                document.getElementById('dropdown').parentNode.removeChild(document.getElementById('dropdown'));
        }
    }

    function resize() {
        var _w = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth;
        if ((typeof oldIE !== 'undefined' || _w >= 920) && window.querySelector) {
            m_resize_menu();
        }
    }
    m_bindEvent(window, 'load', resize);
    m_bindEvent(window, 'resize', resize);
    //window.onresize = resize;
    //window.onload = resize;
</script>

<script>
    function checkSearch() {
        if ($('#ctl00_cphMainContent_Header_m_tbMotsCles').val() == 'Parmi 69151 recettes, 2295 vidéos, 1991 dossiers, 7118 questions' || $('#ctl00_cphMainContent_Header_m_tbMotsCles').val().trim() == '') {
            m_overlay.show({ title: "Recherche", content: "Merci de saisir un mot clé ou le titre d\u0027une recette...", size: "xsmall" });
            return false;
        }
        else {
            recordInternalLinkGA('Recherche', 'Recherche Home', '');
            return true;
        }
    }

    $(".m_bloc_recherche").hover(displayImageHeaderHome, function(){
        $(".m_image_accroche").find("#m_temp_image").stop().animate({ opacity: 0 }, 500, null, function () { $(this).remove() });
		}
	)

    $('.m_carre_titre').click(displayImageHeaderHome);

    function displayImageHeaderHome(){
        var imageAccroche = $(".m_image_accroche");
        if ($(".m_image_accroche").find("#m_temp_image").length == 0) {
            imageAccroche.append("<div id='m_temp_image'></div>");
        }
        imageAccroche.find("#m_temp_image").css({background:"url('https://images.marmitoncdn.org/recipephotos/multiphoto/98/9813ed68-d67b-4090-a4b7-fb2451468401_tn-1500.jpg') no-repeat center center / cover transparent",opacity:0});
			imageAccroche.find("#m_temp_image").stop().animate({ opacity: 1 }, 500);
    }

        function resizeHeaderHome() {
            $('.m_bloc_recherche').addClass('skin_in');
        }

<script type="text/javascript">
function WM_next(eleClick) {
    var ele = $(eleClick).parent().parent().parent();
    var WM_currentSel = $(ele).find(".imgBloc:visible").attr("id");
    WM_currentSel = parseInt(WM_currentSel.substring(WM_currentSel.length - 1));
    if (WM_currentSel <= 2) {
        WM_currentSel += 1;
    } else {
        WM_currentSel = 1;
    }
    WM_refreshRecipe(ele, WM_currentSel);
}

function WM_prev(eleClick) {
    var ele = $(eleClick).parent().parent().parent();
    var WM_currentSel = $(ele).find(".imgBloc:visible").attr("id");
    WM_currentSel = parseInt(WM_currentSel.substring(WM_currentSel.length - 1));
    if (WM_currentSel >= 2) {
        WM_currentSel -= 1;
    } else {
        WM_currentSel = 3;
    }
    WM_refreshRecipe(ele, WM_currentSel);
}

function WM_refreshRecipe(ele, currentSel) {
            
    $(ele).find(".imgBloc").hide();
    $(ele).find(".imgBloc" + currentSel).show();

    $(ele).find(".m_type_plat li").hide();
    $(ele).find(".m_type_plat" + currentSel).show();

    $(ele).find(".m_titre_bloc_flottant").hide();
    $(ele).find(".m_titleBloc" + currentSel).show();

    $(ele).find(".m_partage_bloc_flottant").hide();
    $(ele).find(".m_partage_bloc_flottant" + currentSel).show();
}

function fixedHeightBloc(ele) {
    var maxHeight = 0;
    if(!$(ele).parent().parent().hasClass("m_bloc_hidden")){
        $(ele).parent().parent().show();
    }
    $(ele).parent().find(".imgBloc").each(function () {
        if ($(this).height() > maxHeight) {
            maxHeight = $(this).height();
        }
    });
    $(ele).parent().height(maxHeight);
    $(ele).parent().parent().find(".m_bloc_type_plat").css('margin-top', maxHeight - $(ele).parent().parent().find('.m_type_plat').height() -34);
        
    maxHeight = 0;
    $(ele).parent().parent().find(".m_titre_bloc_flottant").each(function () {
        $(this).css({ height: "auto" });
        if ($(this).height() > maxHeight) {
            maxHeight = $(this).height();
        }
    });
    $(ele).parent().parent().find(".m_titre_bloc_flottant").height(maxHeight+40);
}

function refreshWeekMenuBloc(){
    $(".m_bloc_flottant_type_3").each(function(){
        fixedHeightBloc($(this).find(".imgBloc")[0]); 
    });
}
</script>

                function sendNewUserToNL(email) {
                    try {
                        var chkNLDaily = document.getElementById("m_inscription_checkbox_nl_daily"),
                            chkNLWeekly = document.getElementById("m_inscription_checkbox_nl_weekly"),
                            params = "siteid=1&email=" + email;

                        if (chkNLDaily != undefined &&
                                !chkNLDaily.checked
                                
                                &&
                                chkNLWeekly != undefined &&
                                !chkNLWeekly.checked
                            
                        ) {
                            AddClass(document.getElementById('m_msg_err_add_nl'), "m_open");
                        } else {
                            removeClass(document.getElementById('m_msg_err_add_nl'), "m_open");
                            if (chkNLDaily != undefined && chkNLDaily.checked) {
                                params += "&daily=1";
                            }
                            if (chkNLWeekly != undefined && chkNLWeekly.checked) {
                                params += "&weekly=1";
                            }

                            $.ajax({
                                url: '/Handlers/HInsertNL.ashx',
                                type: "POST",
                                data: params,
                                success: function(data) {
                                    removeClass(document.getElementById('m_form_add_weekly'), "m_form_erreur");
                                    m_overlay.close();
                                    var opts = JSON.parse(data);
                                    m_overlay.show(opts);
                                },
                                error: function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                                    AddClass(document.getElementById('m_form_add_weekly'), "m_form_erreur");
                                    document.getElementById('m_msg_error_add_wk')
                                        .innerHTML =
                                        'Une erreur est survenue.';
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    } catch (ex) {

                    }
                }
            </script>

        filter:0,
        pageHistory:0,
        countObjWaitLoaded:0,
        heightContent:0,
        refreshInProgress:false,
        onLoading:false,
        tryWaitObj:0,
        domainName: 'marmiton.org',
        init: function(){
            $(".m_bloc_flottant_add").remove();
            m_lstBloc.pageHistory = 0;
            m_lstBloc.countObjWaitLoaded = 0;
            m_lstBloc.filter = 0;
            m_lstBloc.onLoading = false;
            m_lstBloc.tryWaitObj = 0;
            setTimeout(function(){m_lstBloc.refresh(false)},100);
            m_lstBloc.heightContent = $('#m_liste_contenus').height();
            $(".m_contenu .m_plus_contenu").show().css({opacity:1});
        },
        refresh: function(autoResize){
            if(m_lstBloc.refreshInProgress == false)
            {
                
                if(m_lstBloc.countObjWaitLoaded > 0 &&  m_lstBloc.tryWaitObj < 50){
                    m_lstBloc.tryWaitObj++;
                    setTimeout(function(){ m_lstBloc.refresh(autoResize);},100);
                }else{
                    $(".m_contenu .m_plus_contenu").removeClass("acBusy");
                    if(autoResize == undefined){
                        autoResize = true;
                    }
                    m_lstBloc.refreshInProgress = true;
                    var valeurOffset = 20;
                    $("#m_liste_contenus li.m_bloc_sas").each(function(){
                        if($(this).children().css("display") == "none"){
                            $(this).addClass("m_bloc_pub_hidden");
                        }else{
                            $(this).removeClass("m_bloc_pub_hidden");
                        }
                    });

                    $('#m_liste_contenus li.m_bloc_flottant:not(.m_bloc_hidden):not(.m_bloc_pub_hidden)').wookmark({
                        autoResize: true,
                        container: $('#m_liste_contenus'),
                        offset: valeurOffset
                    });
                    if(m_lstBloc.heightContent != 0 && autoResize){
                        var lstHeightNew = $('#m_liste_contenus').height();
                        $('#m_liste_contenus').height(m_lstBloc.heightContent);
                        $('#m_liste_contenus').stop().animate({height:lstHeightNew+"px"},2000,function(){
                            
                            m_lstBloc.heightContent = $('#m_liste_contenus').height();
                        });
                        m_lstBloc.refreshInProgress = false;
                    }else{
                        m_lstBloc.refreshInProgress = false;
                    }
                    setTimeout(function(){$('#m_liste_contenus li.m_bloc_flottant:not(.m_bloc_hidden)').animate({opacity:1},500);},100);
                }
            }
         },
        changeFilter:function(idFilter){
            if(idFilter != 0){  
                $(".m_texte_voir_toutes_categories").css({"display":"block"});
                $("#m_liste_contenus .m_bloc_flottant").hide().addClass("m_bloc_hidden");
                $("#m_liste_contenus .m_bloc_flottant_type_"+idFilter).show().removeClass("m_bloc_hidden");
                if(idFilter == 13){
                    $("#m_liste_contenus .m_bloc_flottant_type_14").show().removeClass("m_bloc_hidden");
                }
                m_lstBloc.init();
                m_lstBloc.filter = idFilter;
                m_lstBloc.getPreviousBloc();
            }else{
                $(".m_texte_voir_toutes_categories").css({"display":""});
                $("#m_liste_contenus .m_bloc_flottant").show().removeClass("m_bloc_hidden");
                m_lstBloc.init();
                $(".m_bloc_pub_hidden").hide();
                if(m_lstBloc.heightContent == 0){
                    m_lstBloc.heightContent = 1;
                }
                m_lstBloc.refresh(true);
            }
         },
         getPreviousBloc:function(){
             if(!m_lstBloc.onLoading){
                 m_lstBloc.onLoading = true;
                 $(".m_contenu .m_plus_contenu").addClass("acBusy");
                 var handler = '/Handlers/Headline/HeadlineBloc.ashx';
                 var params = "";
                 if(m_lstBloc.filter != 0)
                     params += "&typebloc="+m_lstBloc.filter;
                 if(this.pageHistory == 1){
                     params += "&start="+this.pageHistory*11;
                 }else{
                     params += "&start="+this.pageHistory*12;
                 }
                 params += "&ph=home"; 
                 mAjax("POST", handler, params, true, this.loadNewContentByResponseAjax, false, "","","", false);
             }
         },
        loadNewContentByResponseAjax:function(data){
            if(data.responseText != null){
                var lstResult =eval("(" + data.responseText + ")");
                if(lstResult == undefined){
                    eval("this.lstResult =(" + data.responseText + ")");
                }
                if(lstResult.key <= 0)
                    $(".m_contenu .m_plus_contenu").animate({opacity:0},500,function(){$(".m_contenu .m_plus_contenu").hide();});
                else
                    var lstHeightOld = $('#m_liste_contenus').height($('#m_liste_contenus').height());
                

                
                m_lstBloc.countObjWaitLoaded = lstResult.value.length;;
                var menuWeekTab = {menu1:null,menu2:null,menu3:null};
                for(var i = 0; i < lstResult.value.length; i++){
                    if(lstResult.value[i].BlocType == 3){
                        switch (lstResult.value[i].DisplayOrder) {
                            case 1:
                                menuWeekTab.menu1 = lstResult.value[i];
                                break;
                            case 2:
                                menuWeekTab.menu2 = lstResult.value[i];
                                break;
                            case 3:
                                menuWeekTab.menu3 = lstResult.value[i];
                                break;
                            default:
        
                        }
                        if(menuWeekTab.menu1 != null && menuWeekTab.menu2 != null && menuWeekTab.menu3 != null){
                            m_lstBloc.addBlocMenuWeek(menuWeekTab.menu1,menuWeekTab.menu2,menuWeekTab.menu3,i*500);
                            menuWeekTab = {menu1:null,menu2:null,menu3:null};
                        }
                    }else{
                        m_lstBloc.addBloc(lstResult.value[i],i*500);
                    }
                }
                if(menuWeekTab.menu1 != null)
                    m_lstBloc.countObjWaitLoaded -= 1;
                if(menuWeekTab.menu2 != null)
                    m_lstBloc.countObjWaitLoaded -= 1;
                if(menuWeekTab.menu3 != null)
                    m_lstBloc.countObjWaitLoaded -= 1;
                m_lstBloc.tryWaitObj = 0;
                m_lstBloc.pageHistory += 1;
                m_lstBloc.refresh(true)
            }
            m_lstBloc.onLoading = false;
        },
        addBloc: function(bloc,timeout){
            var oldBloc = '<li class="m_bloc_flottant m_bloc_flottant_type_'+bloc.BlocType+' rad16 m_bloc_flottant_add" >';
            oldBloc += m_lstBloc.openAnchor(bloc.Url);
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_icone_recette abso '+bloc.CssIcon+'"></div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_image_bloc_flottant">';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_cartouche"></div>';
            oldBloc += '<img src="'+bloc.UrlImage+'" onload="m_lstBloc.removeWaitLoaded();" />';
            oldBloc += '</div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_contenu_bloc_flottant">';
            if(bloc.IsSponsorised){
                oldBloc += '<div class="m_texte_sponso" >Sponsorisé</div>';
                    }
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_titre_bloc_flottant '+bloc.CssTxtColor+'"><div>'+bloc.Title+'</div>'+bloc.Description+'</div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_type_bloc_flottant '+bloc.CssBgColor+'"> ';
            oldBloc += '<div></div>';
            oldBloc += bloc.BlocTypeLabelRessourceKey;
            oldBloc += '</div>';
            if(bloc.HasShare){
                oldBloc += '<div class="m_partage_bloc_flottant">';
                oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+bloc.UrlShareFacebook+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_facebook"></a>';
                oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+bloc.UrlShareTwitter+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_twitter"></a>';
                oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+bloc.UrlShareGooglePlus+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_google"></a>';
                if(bloc.UrlSharePinterest != '')
                    oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+bloc.UrlSharePinterest+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_pinterest"></a>';
                oldBloc += '</div>';
            }
            oldBloc += '</div>';
            oldBloc += '</a></li>';
            $('#m_liste_contenus').append($(oldBloc).css({opacity:0}));
        },
        addBlocMenuWeek: function(menu1,menu2,menu3,timeout){
            var oldBloc = '<li class="m_bloc_flottant m_bloc_flottant_type_'+menu1.BlocType+' rad16 m_bloc_flottant_add">';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_icone_recette abso '+menu1.CssIcon+'"></div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_image_bloc_flottant">';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_cartouche"></div>';
            oldBloc += ' <div class="m_bloc_type_plat">';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_type_plat_fleche_gauche"  onclick="WM_prev(this);"></div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_type_plat">';
            oldBloc += '<ul>';
            oldBloc += '<li class="m_type_plat1"  style="display:none;" >Entrée</li>';
            oldBloc += '<li class="m_type_plat2"  >Plat</li>';
            oldBloc += '<li class="m_type_plat3"  style="display:none;" >Dessert</li>';
            oldBloc += '</ul>';
            oldBloc += '</div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_type_plat_fleche_droite" onclick="WM_next(this);"></div>';
            oldBloc += '</div>';
            oldBloc += '<img id="imgBloc1" src="'+menu1.UrlImage+'" class="imgBloc imgBloc1" onload="fixedHeightBloc(this);m_lstBloc.removeWaitLoaded();"  style="display:none;" />';
            oldBloc += '<img id="imgBloc2" src="'+menu2.UrlImage+'" class="imgBloc imgBloc2" onload="fixedHeightBloc(this);m_lstBloc.removeWaitLoaded();"  />';
            oldBloc += '<img id="imgBloc3" src="'+menu3.UrlImage+'" class="imgBloc imgBloc3" onload="fixedHeightBloc(this);m_lstBloc.removeWaitLoaded();"  style="display:none;" />';

            oldBloc += '</div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_contenu_bloc_flottant">';
            if(menu1.isSponsorised){
                oldBloc += '<dic class="m_texte_sponso" >Sponsorisé</div>';
            }
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_titre_bloc_flottant '+menu1.CssTxtColor+' m_titleBloc1"  style="display:none;" >'+m_lstBloc.openAnchor(menu1.Url)+'<div>'+menu1.Title+'</div>'+menu1.Description+'</a></div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_titre_bloc_flottant '+menu1.CssTxtColor+' m_titleBloc2"  >'+m_lstBloc.openAnchor(menu2.Url)+'<div>'+menu2.Title+'</div>'+menu2.Description+'</a></div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_titre_bloc_flottant '+menu1.CssTxtColor+' m_titleBloc3"  style="display:none;" >'+m_lstBloc.openAnchor(menu3.Url)+'<div>'+menu3.Title+'</div>'+menu3.Description+'</a></div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_type_bloc_flottant '+menu1.CssBgColor+'"> ';
            oldBloc += '<div></div>';
            oldBloc += '<a herf="/recettes/menu-de-la-semaine.aspx">'+menu1.BlocTypeLabelRessourceKey+'</a>';
            oldBloc += '</div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_partage_bloc_flottant m_partage_bloc_flottant1"  style="display:none;" >';
            oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+menu1.UrlShareFacebook+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_facebook"></a>';
            oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+menu1.UrlShareTwitter+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_twitter"></a>';
            oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+menu1.UrlShareGooglePlus+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_google"></a>';
            if(menu1.UrlSharePinterest != '')
                oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+menu1.UrlSharePinterest+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_pinterest"></a>';
            oldBloc += '</div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_partage_bloc_flottant m_partage_bloc_flottant2"  >';
            oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+menu2.UrlShareFacebook+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_facebook"></a>';
            oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+menu2.UrlShareTwitter+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_twitter"></a>';
            oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+menu2.UrlShareGooglePlus+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_google"></a>';
            if(menu2.UrlSharePinterest != '')
                oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+menu2.UrlSharePinterest+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_pinterest"></a>';
            oldBloc += '</div>';
            oldBloc += '<div class="m_partage_bloc_flottant m_partage_bloc_flottant3"  style="display:none;" >';
            oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+menu3.UrlShareFacebook+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_facebook"></a>';
            oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+menu3.UrlSharePinterest+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_twitter"></a>';
            oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+menu3.UrlShareGooglePlus+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_google"></a>';
            if(menu3.UrlSharePinterest != '')
                oldBloc += '<a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="popupOpen(\''+menu3.UrlSharePinterest+'\',\'share\',600,400);return false;" class="m_partage_pinterest"></a>';
            oldBloc += '</div>';
            oldBloc += '</div>';
            oldBloc += '</li>';
            $('#m_liste_contenus').append($(oldBloc).css({opacity:0}));
        },
        removeWaitLoaded:function(){
            m_lstBloc.countObjWaitLoaded--;
            if(m_lstBloc.countObjWaitLoaded <= 0){
                setTimeout(function(){m_lstBloc.refresh(true)},100);
            }
        },
        refreshScreenChange:function(){
            setTimeout(function(){m_lstBloc.refresh(true)},100);
        },
        extractDomain:function(url){
            var domain;
            if (url.indexOf("://") > -1 || url.indexOf("//") == 0) {
                domain = url.split('/')[2];
            } else {
                domain = url.split('/')[0];
            }
            return domain.split(':')[0];
        },
        isDomainInternal:function(domain) {
            if (domain == '' || domain.indexOf(m_lstBloc.domainName) > -1)
                return true;
            return false;
        },
        openAnchor:function(url){
            var anchor = '<a href="'+ url+'"' + (m_lstBloc.isDomainInternal(m_lstBloc.extractDomain(url)) ? '' : ' target="_blank"') + '>';
            return anchor;
        }
    };

    $(document).ready(new function () {
        m_lstBloc.init();
        m_bindEvent(window, 'resize', m_lstBloc.refreshScreenChange);
        m_bindEvent(window, 'resize', refreshWeekMenuBloc);

        if (window.location.hash == '#m_sondage')
            setTimeout(function() {$(window).scrollTop($('#m_sondage').position().top + $('#haut_page').height() + $('.m_header').height());}, 200);
    });    
</script>
